      • getAdvLastAccrDte

        public TField getAdvLastAccrDte()
        Returns the AdvLastAccrDte

        Field description: A system-maintained, no-input field which is only utilised where SAFECUSTODY.VALUES>PERFORM.ACCRUAL forCharge.Type 'IC' is set to DAILY. While Advisory charges are being accrued on a daily basis (via 'F' entries) this field holds the start date ofthe accrual period. Once the charges are approved, real accounting entries replace the accrual entries and the datein this field is moved on to the start of the next charge period. Because the date in this field is static until after the charges are approved, it is unaffected by the Close OfBusiness (COB) which runs on the day that the Advisory charge falls due and it can therefore be used to communicatea consistent charge period start date to core accounting (the COB which runs on the charge frequency date updatesboth SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFE.LAST.RUN and SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFECUSTODY.FREQ so these fields cannot be used for thepurpose).

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AdvLastAccrDte

      • getCheckLimit

        public TField getCheckLimit()
        Returns the CheckLimit

        Field description: Input is only accepted for accounts where the DEALER.BOOK field is populated, i.e. the banks own books where asecurities trading position is maintained. A value of 'Y' indicates that Limits should be checked for all security trades for this book where theSECURITY.MASTER record has the LIMIT.REF field populated. On first input of 'Y' limits will be checked and updated for all relevant trades on this book, when the recordis authorised. If this field is changed and was previously set to 'Y' then limits will be backed out for all trades on thisbook, when the record is authorised. Validation Rules: One character of 'Y', 'N' or null. Optional Input. DEALER.BOOK must be populated.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CheckLimit

      • getCleanBookCost

        public TField getCleanBookCost()
        Returns the CleanBookCost

        Field description: Indicates whether the amount traded is the amount traded plus costs to be posted to CRF. The Y or NO flag determines how the amount to be posted to the customers account is to be calculated. If flag isset to "Y" then the Gross amount Traded is the amount posted. If Flag is "NO" then the Gross amount Traded plus anycommissions and fees is the amount posted. Validation Rules: Y or NO are accepted as valid input (Optional input) Input is mandatory only if the portfolio is a dealer book.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CleanBookCost

      • getClosureDate

        public TField getClosureDate()
        Returns the ClosureDate

        Field description: The date when the Security Account is to be closed. N.B. This date can not be changed once authorised. If a date is entered in this field then the Safekeeping Charges and Management fees will be calculated andposted on that date. If no account has been set in the SAFEKEEP.CHARG.ACC field then an override is issued stating FEES WILL BE POSTED TO SUSPENSE. However if there has are any unposted Outstanding Safekeeping Charges or Management Fees then an Override message of SAFE CUSTODY FEES NOT POSTED or MANAGEMENT FEES NOT POSTED is produced. An override message of NO ACCOUNTS ON PORTFOLIO will be generated if CLOSURE.DATE is entered and the ACCOUNT.NOS field is null. The system checks to see if there are any unsettled Corporate Action Entitlements, unsettled Trades or unsettled Transfers In of Stock then the system issues an override of UNSETTLED TRANSACTION followed by the transaction key. The system also checks for the following cases and issues Overrides when there is an Outstanding Corporate Actions on the closing Portfolio OUTSTANDING CORPORATE ACTION followed by the transaction key Outstanding Orders on the closing Portfolio OUTSTANDING ORDER followed by the transaction key. Unauthorised SEC.TRADE, SECURITY.TRANSFER or DIARY UNAUTHORISED TRANSACTION followed by the transaction key. Or OUTSTANDING CORPORATE ACTION followed by the transaction key. Validation Rules: Standard date format. (Optional input) No change field

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The ClosureDate

      • getCntRealPlCatLo

        public TField getCntRealPlCatLo()
        Returns the CntRealPlCatLo

        Field description: This field represents the Category to which Contingent Loss entries will be posted till the value date. For aFoward dated Dealer Book trade, which has a Loss attached to it, an entry will be raised only on the Value Date. (When the field TRADE.SETTLE.ACCTG is set as 'SETTLEMENT' in SC.STD.SEC.TRADE) This functionality will enable posting of the Loss on the Trade to this Contingent bucket until value date whenthe entry will be reversed and the Loss will be posted to the original bucket. Validation Rules: VALID INPUT - Profit and Loss categories between 52-000 and 59-999 INPUT allowed only if the Portfolio is an own Book Portfolio and the field POST.CONT.REAL.PL is set to 'YES' inSC.STD.SEC.TRADE

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CntRealPlCatLo

      • getCntRealPlCatPr

        public TField getCntRealPlCatPr()
        Returns the CntRealPlCatPr

        Field description: This field represents the Category to which Contingent Profit entries have to be posted till the value date. For a forward dated Dealer book Trade which has a profit attached to it, an entry will be raised only on theValue Date. (When the field TRADE.SETTLE.ACCTG is set as "SETTLEMENT" in SC.STD.SEC.TRADE) This functionality will enable posting of the profit on the Trade to this Contingent bucket until value datewhen the entry will be reversed and the profit will be posted to the original bucket. Validation Rules: VALID INPUT - Profit and Loss categories between 52-000 and 59-999 INPUT allowed only if the Portfolio is an own Book Portfolio and the field POST.CONT.REAL.PL is set to "YES" inSC.STD.SEC.TRADE

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CntRealPlCatPr

      • getDiscsoldToRealpl

        public TField getDiscsoldToRealpl()
        Returns the DiscsoldToRealpl

        Field description: Flag for posting discount accrued, which has been sold, to realised P & L. When a sale transaction is entered, if any discount has been accrued/amortised prior to the sale, then aproportion of this amount is calculated based on the quantity sold over the stock purchased. This amount will then be debited from the discount provision P & L and the Realised P & L will becredited if this field is set to "Y". Validation Rules: "Y", "NO" or Null may be entered. (Optional input) This field becomes mandatory if this is a dealer book portfolio, otherwise it must be kept null.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The DiscsoldToRealpl

      • getMisInterestRate

        public TField getMisInterestRate()
        Returns the MisInterestRate

        Field description: Identifies the refinancing rate for the corresponding transaction. It will be used to determine the Management Information System (M.I.S) Customer Profitability Analysis. Thus the User should input the rate at the contract level when the individual refinancing rate is available. This would be the case, for example, for contracts which have been MATCHED or for contracts where the Marketing Department has agreed with the Treasury Department on a particular Cost-of-Funds Rate. The rate will be entered as a FIXED Interest Rate Type. It should normally be greater than the contract interest rate for Deposits and smaller than the contract interest rate for Placements. The system will use the Pool Rate when this field and the M.I.S. INTEREST KEY field are not present. Note: Default means that no input was made in the M.I.S. INTEREST KEY nor in the M.I.S. Interest Rate. The input will be entered in the M.I.S. Interest Key or in the M.I.S. Interest Rate depending on whether the User wants to input an interest key or a rate. This field may be changed at any time during the life of the contract but will take effect from the current month unless accruals had not yet been performed on the particular contract (back-value initiation). __________________________________________________ (1) 1 to 10 Numeric characters plus a decimal point (Standard rate format 6.9). (Optional input; Default value = None). (2) Input in this field will only be accepted if the M.I.S. Interest key was left blank. (3) Input will also be accepted for the account receivable and sundry contract types.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The MisInterestRate

Validation Rules: 0 - 12 Alphabetic characters (Mandatory input if DEALER BOOK entered otherwise not allowed) The user can only input a value in this field if the portfolio is a DEALER.BOOK portfolio.       • getPostDiscUpfront

        public TField getPostDiscUpfront()
        Returns the PostDiscUpfront

        Field description: Indicates whether or not discount is to be posted upfront. "Y" means discount amount is posted upfront. "NO" means that discount amount is treated as a normal interestaccrual. Upfront methodology requires the underlying assets to be grossed up to par/face value. It is possible to post discounts and premiums upfront without daily accruals taking place. If discount is not posted upfront and discount accrued, then on maturity date a fictitious sale is assumed topost the discount accrued. Validation Rules: Y or NO are accepted as valid input. (Optional input) Input is mandatory if portfolio is a dealer book.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The PostDiscUpfront

      • getPostUnrealPl

        public TField getPostUnrealPl()
        Returns the PostUnrealPl

        Field description: Defines whether post unrealised profits and/or loss for this portfolio are to be posted. This flag indicates how unrealised profit and losses for this own book portfolio is to be handled. Value "BOTH" means that unrealised profits and unrealised losses are to be posted. Value "LOSS" means that unrealised losses are to be posted, while unrealised profits are not posted. Value "RVAL" means that unrealised losses are to be posted using the REVALUATION.PRICE held on theSC.TRADING.POSITION (the lowest recorded market price) Value "LOWER.COST" indicates that the underlying position will always be carried at either the cost price ormarket price - whichever is lowest. Value "NONE" means that unrealised profits and unrealised loss are not to be posted. Validation Rules: Input only allowed for DEALER.BOOK portfolios Only "BOTH", "LOSS", "RVAL", "LOWER.COST" or "NONE" can be entered in this field. If REVALUATION is "NO" then this field must be "NONE". If REVALUATION is "Y" then this field must be "BOTH", "RVAL", "LOWER.COST" or "LOSS"

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The PostUnrealPl

        Returns the PpAdjFactor

        Field description: Percentage applied on buying power to calculate the actual Buying power. Can be set only if field BUYING.POWER in OV.PARAMETER is set to YES. Cannot be set if MARGIN.LENDING is set toYES.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The PpAdjFactor

        public TField getRevalFreq()
        Returns the RevalFreq

        Field description: Indicates the frequency required to revalue the trading positions. Revaluation of the banks own portfolio trading positions will be carried out based on the frequency entered.This may be daily, weekly, monthly or yearly. Accounting entries will be generated during the batch run, to postunrealised P/L entries based on current prices from the Security Master. This will be rolled over at the requestedfrequency. Validation Rules: 17 characters frequency code. Valid inputs are: B - Bank business date D - Daily W - Weekly T - Each twelfth month (year end) M - Monthly Input only allowed if the portfolio is a Dealer Book portfolio with REVALUATION set to "Y".

        public TField getRevalPostMethod()
        Returns the RevalPostMethod

        Field description: Defines the portfolio unrealised revaluation posting method. Two different methods can be adopted in posting the reval amounts. 1. Reverse previous day reval amount &Post current day's reval . 2. Post only the difference in previous days reval and current day's reval amount. Thereare 2 different methods under ADJ, i) If the unrealised profit & loss categories are diff. ii) If thecategories are same. Validation Rules: Valid values are null, I/O & ADJ. If null or I/O posting is done as in 1 explained above. If ADJ, posting isas explained in 2. The user can only input a value in this field if the portfolio is a DEALER.BOOK portfolio.

      • getSafeLastAccrDte

        public TField getSafeLastAccrDte()
        Returns the SafeLastAccrDte

        Field description: A system-maintained, no-input field which is only utilised where SAFECUSTODY.VALUES>PERFORM.ACCRUAL forCharge.Type 'SC' is set to DAILY. While Safekeeping charges are being accrued on a daily basis (via 'F' entries) this field holds the start dateof the accrual period. Once the charges are approved, real accounting entries replace the accrual entries and thedate in this field is moved on to the start of the next charge period. Because the date in this field is static until after the charges are approved, it is unaffected by the Close OfBusiness (COB) which runs on the day that the Safekeeping charge falls due and it can therefore be used tocommunicate a consistent charge period start date to core accounting (the COB which runs on the charge frequencydate updates both SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFE.LAST.RUN and SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFECUSTODY.FREQ so these fields cannot beused for the purpose).

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The SafeLastAccrDte

      • setAdvLastAccrDte

        public void setAdvLastAccrDte(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AdvLastAccrDte
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: A system-maintained, no-input field which is only utilised where SAFECUSTODY.VALUES>PERFORM.ACCRUAL forCharge.Type 'IC' is set to DAILY. While Advisory charges are being accrued on a daily basis (via 'F' entries) this field holds the start date ofthe accrual period. Once the charges are approved, real accounting entries replace the accrual entries and the datein this field is moved on to the start of the next charge period. Because the date in this field is static until after the charges are approved, it is unaffected by the Close OfBusiness (COB) which runs on the day that the Advisory charge falls due and it can therefore be used to communicatea consistent charge period start date to core accounting (the COB which runs on the charge frequency date updatesboth SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFE.LAST.RUN and SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFECUSTODY.FREQ so these fields cannot be used for thepurpose).

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The date of the next calculation of Advisory Fees for this portfolio and frequency to be used in defining thesubsequent Advisory Fees Runs. Input is only allowed if the calculation frequency for Advisory Fees is defined at a portfolio level (i.e. theCOMPANY.CALC field on SAFECUSTODY.VALUES associated with a CHARGE.TYPE of 'IC' is set to 'N'). Otherwise the valuein this field will be taken from the CHARGE.FREQ field on the SAFECUSTODY.VALUES record for the company associatedwith a chanrge type of 'iC'. This field consists of two components as follows - 1) Next Statement Date: 1-9 Date characters. The default value calculated by the system depending on thefrequency. 2) Frequency: 1-5 type SS (uppercase alpha or numeric, first character alpha) characters. Validation Rules: Input only allowed for Customer portfolios in the COMPANY.CALC flag is set to 'NO'. Standard T24 frequency field. Any frequency input must be a monthly frequency.

      • setClosureDate

        public void setClosureDate(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for ClosureDate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The date when the Security Account is to be closed. N.B. This date can not be changed once authorised. If a date is entered in this field then the Safekeeping Charges and Management fees will be calculated andposted on that date. If no account has been set in the SAFEKEEP.CHARG.ACC field then an override is issued stating FEES WILL BE POSTED TO SUSPENSE. However if there has are any unposted Outstanding Safekeeping Charges or Management Fees then an Override message of SAFE CUSTODY FEES NOT POSTED or MANAGEMENT FEES NOT POSTED is produced. An override message of NO ACCOUNTS ON PORTFOLIO will be generated if CLOSURE.DATE is entered and the ACCOUNT.NOS field is null. The system checks to see if there are any unsettled Corporate Action Entitlements, unsettled Trades or unsettled Transfers In of Stock then the system issues an override of UNSETTLED TRANSACTION followed by the transaction key. The system also checks for the following cases and issues Overrides when there is an Outstanding Corporate Actions on the closing Portfolio OUTSTANDING CORPORATE ACTION followed by the transaction key Outstanding Orders on the closing Portfolio OUTSTANDING ORDER followed by the transaction key. Unauthorised SEC.TRADE, SECURITY.TRANSFER or DIARY UNAUTHORISED TRANSACTION followed by the transaction key. Or OUTSTANDING CORPORATE ACTION followed by the transaction key. Validation Rules: Standard date format. (Optional input) No change field

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setClosureDate

        public void setClosureDate(TField value)
        Set the specified value for ClosureDate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The date when the Security Account is to be closed. N.B. This date can not be changed once authorised. If a date is entered in this field then the Safekeeping Charges and Management fees will be calculated andposted on that date. If no account has been set in the SAFEKEEP.CHARG.ACC field then an override is issued stating FEES WILL BE POSTED TO SUSPENSE. However if there has are any unposted Outstanding Safekeeping Charges or Management Fees then an Override message of SAFE CUSTODY FEES NOT POSTED or MANAGEMENT FEES NOT POSTED is produced. An override message of NO ACCOUNTS ON PORTFOLIO will be generated if CLOSURE.DATE is entered and the ACCOUNT.NOS field is null. The system checks to see if there are any unsettled Corporate Action Entitlements, unsettled Trades or unsettled Transfers In of Stock then the system issues an override of UNSETTLED TRANSACTION followed by the transaction key. The system also checks for the following cases and issues Overrides when there is an Outstanding Corporate Actions on the closing Portfolio OUTSTANDING CORPORATE ACTION followed by the transaction key Outstanding Orders on the closing Portfolio OUTSTANDING ORDER followed by the transaction key. Unauthorised SEC.TRADE, SECURITY.TRANSFER or DIARY UNAUTHORISED TRANSACTION followed by the transaction key. Or OUTSTANDING CORPORATE ACTION followed by the transaction key. Validation Rules: Standard date format. (Optional input) No change field

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCntRealPlCatLo

        public void setCntRealPlCatLo(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for CntRealPlCatLo
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field represents the Category to which Contingent Loss entries will be posted till the value date. For aFoward dated Dealer Book trade, which has a Loss attached to it, an entry will be raised only on the Value Date. (When the field TRADE.SETTLE.ACCTG is set as 'SETTLEMENT' in SC.STD.SEC.TRADE) This functionality will enable posting of the Loss on the Trade to this Contingent bucket until value date whenthe entry will be reversed and the Loss will be posted to the original bucket. Validation Rules: VALID INPUT - Profit and Loss categories between 52-000 and 59-999 INPUT allowed only if the Portfolio is an own Book Portfolio and the field POST.CONT.REAL.PL is set to 'YES' inSC.STD.SEC.TRADE

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setDiscsoldToRealpl

        public void setDiscsoldToRealpl(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for DiscsoldToRealpl
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Flag for posting discount accrued, which has been sold, to realised P & L. When a sale transaction is entered, if any discount has been accrued/amortised prior to the sale, then aproportion of this amount is calculated based on the quantity sold over the stock purchased. This amount will then be debited from the discount provision P & L and the Realised P & L will becredited if this field is set to "Y". Validation Rules: "Y", "NO" or Null may be entered. (Optional input) This field becomes mandatory if this is a dealer book portfolio, otherwise it must be kept null.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setMisInterestRate

        public void setMisInterestRate(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for MisInterestRate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the refinancing rate for the corresponding transaction. It will be used to determine the Management Information System (M.I.S) Customer Profitability Analysis. Thus the User should input the rate at the contract level when the individual refinancing rate is available. This would be the case, for example, for contracts which have been MATCHED or for contracts where the Marketing Department has agreed with the Treasury Department on a particular Cost-of-Funds Rate. The rate will be entered as a FIXED Interest Rate Type. It should normally be greater than the contract interest rate for Deposits and smaller than the contract interest rate for Placements. The system will use the Pool Rate when this field and the M.I.S. INTEREST KEY field are not present. Note: Default means that no input was made in the M.I.S. INTEREST KEY nor in the M.I.S. Interest Rate. The input will be entered in the M.I.S. Interest Key or in the M.I.S. Interest Rate depending on whether the User wants to input an interest key or a rate. This field may be changed at any time during the life of the contract but will take effect from the current month unless accruals had not yet been performed on the particular contract (back-value initiation). __________________________________________________ (1) 1 to 10 Numeric characters plus a decimal point (Standard rate format 6.9). (Optional input; Default value = None). (2) Input in this field will only be accepted if the M.I.S. Interest key was left blank. (3) Input will also be accepted for the account receivable and sundry contract types.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setPortfolioFees

        public void setPortfolioFees(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PortfolioFees
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Field indicating whether portfolio fees are calculated automatically, manually or not at all. If this field is set to NONE no Management or Safecustody fees will be calculated for this portfolio. If this field is set to 'MANUAL' then the user will calculate the Management and Safecustody fees manually. If this field is set to 'AUTOMATIC' then the system will automatically calculate the Management and Safecustodyfees on the dates given in the ADVISORY.FREQ and SAFECUSTODY.FREQ fields respectively. Validation Rules: Input only allowed for customer portfolios. Only input of 'AUTOMATIC', 'MANUAL' or 'NONE' allowed. Will default to AUTOMATIC.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

Validation Rules: 0 - 12 Alphabetic characters (Mandatory input if DEALER BOOK entered otherwise not allowed) The user can only input a value in this field if the portfolio is a DEALER.BOOK portfolio.       • setPostDiscUpfront

        public void setPostDiscUpfront(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PostDiscUpfront
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates whether or not discount is to be posted upfront. "Y" means discount amount is posted upfront. "NO" means that discount amount is treated as a normal interestaccrual. Upfront methodology requires the underlying assets to be grossed up to par/face value. It is possible to post discounts and premiums upfront without daily accruals taking place. If discount is not posted upfront and discount accrued, then on maturity date a fictitious sale is assumed topost the discount accrued. Validation Rules: Y or NO are accepted as valid input. (Optional input) Input is mandatory if portfolio is a dealer book.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setPostUnrealPl

        public void setPostUnrealPl(TField value)
        Set the specified value for PostUnrealPl
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines whether post unrealised profits and/or loss for this portfolio are to be posted. This flag indicates how unrealised profit and losses for this own book portfolio is to be handled. Value "BOTH" means that unrealised profits and unrealised losses are to be posted. Value "LOSS" means that unrealised losses are to be posted, while unrealised profits are not posted. Value "RVAL" means that unrealised losses are to be posted using the REVALUATION.PRICE held on theSC.TRADING.POSITION (the lowest recorded market price) Value "LOWER.COST" indicates that the underlying position will always be carried at either the cost price ormarket price - whichever is lowest. Value "NONE" means that unrealised profits and unrealised loss are not to be posted. Validation Rules: Input only allowed for DEALER.BOOK portfolios Only "BOTH", "LOSS", "RVAL", "LOWER.COST" or "NONE" can be entered in this field. If REVALUATION is "NO" then this field must be "NONE". If REVALUATION is "Y" then this field must be "BOTH", "RVAL", "LOWER.COST" or "LOSS"

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setRevalFreq(TField value)
        Set the specified value for RevalFreq
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates the frequency required to revalue the trading positions. Revaluation of the banks own portfolio trading positions will be carried out based on the frequency entered.This may be daily, weekly, monthly or yearly. Accounting entries will be generated during the batch run, to postunrealised P/L entries based on current prices from the Security Master. This will be rolled over at the requestedfrequency. Validation Rules: 17 characters frequency code. Valid inputs are: B - Bank business date D - Daily W - Weekly T - Each twelfth month (year end) M - Monthly Input only allowed if the portfolio is a Dealer Book portfolio with REVALUATION set to "Y".

      • setSafeLastAccrDte

        public void setSafeLastAccrDte(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for SafeLastAccrDte
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: A system-maintained, no-input field which is only utilised where SAFECUSTODY.VALUES>PERFORM.ACCRUAL forCharge.Type 'SC' is set to DAILY. While Safekeeping charges are being accrued on a daily basis (via 'F' entries) this field holds the start dateof the accrual period. Once the charges are approved, real accounting entries replace the accrual entries and thedate in this field is moved on to the start of the next charge period. Because the date in this field is static until after the charges are approved, it is unaffected by the Close OfBusiness (COB) which runs on the day that the Safekeeping charge falls due and it can therefore be used tocommunicate a consistent charge period start date to core accounting (the COB which runs on the charge frequencydate updates both SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFE.LAST.RUN and SEC.ACC.MASTER>SAFECUSTODY.FREQ so these fields cannot beused for the purpose).

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setSafecustodyFreq(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for SafecustodyFreq
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The date of the next calculation of Safecustody Fees for this portfolio and frequency to be used in defining thesubsequent Safecustody Fees Runs. Input is only allowed if the calculation frequency for Safecustody Fees is defined at a portfolio level (i.e.the COMPANY.CALC field on SAFECUSTODY.VALUES associated with a CHARGE.TYPE of 'SC' is set to 'N'). Otherwise thevalue in this field will be taken from the CHARGE.FREQ field on the SAFECUSTODY.VALUES record for the companyassociated with a chanrge type of 'SC'. This field consists of two components as follows - 1) Next Statement Date: 1-9 Date characters. The default value calculated by the system depending on thefrequency. 2) Frequency: 1-5 type SS (uppercase alpha or numeric, first character alpha) characters. Validation Rules: Input only allowed for Customer portfolios in the COMPANY.CALC flag is set to "NO". Standard T24 frequency field. Any frequency input must be a monthly frequency.

        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUnrealPlCatLoss

        public void setUnrealPlCatLoss(TField value)
        Set the specified value for UnrealPlCatLoss
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies the CATEGORY Code to which unrealised loss accounting entries will be posted. If PORTFOLIO.TYPE is set as AVAIL.SALE then an Internal category account is allowed. Otherwise a P/L Category must be specified. Must be in the range 50000 - 59999. If PORTFOLIO.TYPE is set as FVOCI, then only Internal category account (10000-19999) is allowed. This field is mandatory for dealer book if POST.UNREAL.PL is set to BOTH or LOSS otherwise input is not allowed. A dealer book portfolio is a bank's own portfolio and is denoted by an input having been made in the DEALER.BOOKfield. Validation Rules: 5 Numeric characters. Any input made must exist on the CATEGORY file.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUnrealProfitSusp

        public void setUnrealProfitSusp(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for UnrealProfitSusp
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies the CATEGORY code to which the provision for unrealised profits will be posted for this portfolio. Must be in the range 10000 to 19999 Input only valid for Dealer Book portfolios that have revaluation. Validation Rules: Any input must exist on CATEGORY table and be in the range 10000 to 19999 If a value has been entered in the DEALER.BOOK field and the REVALUATION field is set to 'Y' then this field ismandatory otherwise input is not allowed. "DEALER.BOOK" field then a CATEGORY must be entered in this fieldotherwise this field must be left blank. If value is entered then unrealised profits are posted to this provisionaccount, else profit is posted to CRB or ASSET.CAT based on CRF.POST flag in SC.STD.SEC.TRADE Is a NOCHANGE fieldif instruments are traded in this book.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setValuationCurrency

        public void setValuationCurrency(TField value)
        Set the specified value for ValuationCurrency
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the currency in which the valuation reports are printed. When producing the valuation reports, the amounts printed will be converted to this currency if it is present.If the value in this field is null then the reference currency will be used to produce the reports. Validation Rules: 3 characters currency code (Optional input) Must be present on the CURRENCY file.

      • setWrReporting

        public void setWrReporting(TField value)
        Set the specified value for WrReporting
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Denotes whether the WR (Wealth Reporting) product will generate reports for this portfolio or not. If this flagis set, this portfolio will be included in report data generation for WR, otherwise it will be ignored. If the WR module has not been installed for the current company, this flag has no effect, and setting the flagwill generate an appropriate error.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing
